rin chen gter mdzod chen po'i smin grol dkyus gcig tu 'bog pa'i skabs kyi lag len phyogs mtshon dang /
bcas bsham bya ba'i tshul mthong bas go 'byed ces bya ba bzhugs so //
na mo gu ru de ba DA ki nI ye /
byin rlabs rdzogs ldan nor bu'i sprin chen 'khrigs //
dngos grub bdud rtsi'i char rgyun 'dzad med 'jo //
phrin las rin chen snye ma 'dod rgur sbyin //
rtsa gsum chos skyong bcas pas dge legs stsol //
rat+na gram bur spungs pa'i gter mdzod che'i //
smin grol sgo 'phar gtan pa med dbye'i tshe //
lde'u mig 'phrul dang sgron me'i snang byed bzhin //
lag len khrigs chags phyogs mtshon dgod par spro //
dus gsum rgyal ba'i spyi gzugs o rgyan gyi slob dpon chen po mtsho skyes rdo rjes sangs rgyas kyi cho 'phrul chen pos dpal gyi mgur nas chos kyi rnga bo che gdul bya'i khams dbang skal pa dang mthun par bsam yas brjod las 'das par bsgrags par mdzad pa'i /
zab don gyi snying po 'ga' zhig phyis 'byung bod 'bangs la thugs brtses dgongs te mkha' 'gro gtad rgyas btab pa rnams smon lam gyi mthu sad pa'i gter ston sprul      pa'i skyes mchog rnams kyis gnas dus dang 'tshams par bstan 'gro'i dge legs spel ba'i btsas su snang bar mdzad pa ji snyed cig mchis pa las /
rang nyid kyi skal pa bzang po'i dpyid du 'ongs pa rnams kyi smin grol rtsa ba'i skor bstan pa'i sri zhu dang mos ldan re re tsam la'ang phan thogs par re ba'i lhag bsam bzang pos phyogs gcig tu bsdus pa rin chen gter gyi mdzod chen po'i smin grol dkyus gcig tu 'bogs pa'i skabs kyi phyag len mdor bsdus 'god pa la gsum /
spyir ji ltar bya ba'i lag len /
nyer mkho'i yo byad sta gon /
bye brag dbang rnams kyi gshom bkod bstan pa'o //
dang po ni /
'di nyid kyi smin grol bgyid par brtsam pa na /
slob dpon gyis rang gi rtsa ba'i yi dam mam dkyil 'khor spyi'i khyab bdag rdo rje sems dpa' lta bu'i bsnyen pa kha gso zhag bdun gyis nyung mthar byas te gnang ba stsol ba'i gsol ba gdab /
zhu ba po'i slob ma dad pa dam tshig thub nges nyams len dang 'chad spel nus pa bdun nam bcu gsum las mi mang ba khrigs bcad dgos te /
zhi khro rtsa gsum gu ru zhi ba thugs rje chen po sogs khyab gdal du bskur chog kyang zhu mkhan ha cang mang na lcogs thabs med pa dang /
zab gnyan che ba'i rigs phal mo che mang po la bskur mi rung ba 'ga' zhig brgyud 'dzin gcig gam gsum las mi spel bar gsungs pas dbye bsal thog ma nas phyed pa gal che'o //
de nas dbang khrid ma tshugs pa'i snga rol du /
rtsa ba gsum la tshogs skong dang maN+Dal /
chos srung la skong gsol /
sde brgyad la mdos glud /
yul lhar bsang brngan /
mgron bzhir phud mchod spyi gsol /
chu gtor /
gsung rab klog 'don /
sdig sgrib nyams chag sbyong ba yig brgya'i bsgom bzlas /
dong sprugs cho ga
/phyag bskor /
sAts+tsha grangs mang sogs gnang ba zhu zhing bar chad mi 'byung bar /
don gnyis 'grub pa'i rten 'brel gyi dge ba'i dpung bskyed dpon slob thun mong nas ci 'grub tu byas pas gnas skabs bar chad mi 'byung ba dang phyin chad bkra shis pa'i rten 'brel du 'gyur ro //
lag len dngos la rgyas pa sgrub chen gyi khong du btang ba dang /
bsdus pa sgrub chen mi spel ba'i lugs gnyis bla slob 'khos dang longs skabs kyis gang lcogs bya chog cing /
gnyis ka'ang gza' skar dus tshes bzang po zhig la dbu btsugs te rtsa ba'i rgyu dbang bka' brgyad bde gshegs 'dus pa'i dbang chen zhig nges par sngon du 'gro dgos pas /
dang po ltar na /
'brel dang dgos pa'i gnad shin tu che ba'i dbang gis rigs kun khyab bdag dpal rdo rje sems dpa'i sgrub thabs bka' gter zung 'jug smin lugs nyid kyis khog dbub dgos pas /
de'i sgrub khog rnam grol snye ma nas ji ltar 'byung ba bzhin /
nyin dang po'i snga dro sa chog nas mtshams gcod rjes 'brel bcas /
phyi dro lha sta gon dang rgyan bkod 'phros su sgrub thabs 'dod 'jo bum bzang gi dbu nas 'byung ba'i bla ma gsang 'dus zlum po bzhi dbang dang gtor dbang bcas bsham sgrub bskur ba bcas grub par bya /
byin rlabs 'di lta bu dang rjes gnang srog gtad sogs dkyil 'khor chen po'i dbang bzhi yongs rdzogs sngon du ma song ba la sbyin byar min kyang 'di ni chos sgo 'byed pa byin rlabs bla ma'i gtor dbang zhes ched du bsngags pa sogs dmigs su bsal ba'i dgos pa dang ldan pas so //
nyin gnyis par rdor sems sgrub mchod rgyas pa dzab bzlas nyu le skrod cing byin dbab pas mtshon sgrub chen gyi chings ji lta bar bya /
dgong mor nyang gter bka' brgyad bdag bskyed phyag rgya rkyang sgrub tsam byas la sta gon chas bsgrig
/slob ma rnams 'tshogs /
khrus bgegs gtor srung 'khor /
lo rgyus mtshams sbyar lo chen dbang bshad 'khyogs mtshams can nas bka' brgyad kyi bshad pa brjod la maN+Dal 'bul /
mdo byang chen mo ltar bka' brgyad kyi sta gon yongs rdzogs grub par bya /
'di phyin chad yun ring bas bsnyen rgyun 'khyol dka' yang rdor sems sgrub mchod ma chag pa dgos mod /
bla mas longs khyab med cing mi lcogs na gzhan pa'i bla grwa kha shas la nyin re bzhin gong ltar bsgrub bcol /
'di nas brtsam mjug ma grub kyi bar dngos rol rjes 'brang gter srung rnams kyi gtor 'bul nyin re tshar re 'don mkhan zur du yod na legs /
dngos rol tshang ma ma grub na dam can spyi gtor khongs su mngon rtogs gang lcogs re mos btsud /
sgrub gzhi yod pa'i gnas der go yul dogs na khang pa gzhan du mchod gtor rgyas bsdus gang lcogs la brten nas 'don chog go
/dgong mo nas bka' brgyad dbang chas bsham la /
nyin gsum par las byang bde rol gyis bsgrubs la mdo byang chen mo'i dbang rdzogs par bskur /
rjes chog grub nas de'i chas bsdus la kar gling zhi khro'i dbang chas bsham /
nyin bzhi par de'i dbang bskur ba nas brtsam grangs gang thon bya ba las spar bkab med /
rat+na'i tshe sgrub gsang ba 'dus pa'i dbang rjes su bzhag
/dbang khrid yongs rdzogs grub pa'i nyin rdor sems cho ga rgyas par btang zhing sgrub pa'i dngos grub blang ba'i tshe slob dpon gzhan gyis mchog gi sbyin sreg bya zhing /
de nas dbang dang khrid bcas rdzogs par bya /
gtor ma btang ba sogs rjes rim rnams bya /
phyir nyin snga bar tshe gsang dbang chas bsham nas las byang gis bsgrubs la tshe dbang rgyas bsdus rnams kyis mthar dge byas te de'i rjes chog dang /
sgrub pa'i tho 'grol sogs sgrub khog las 'byung ba ltar mtha' rgyas su bya ba yin no //
gnyis pa spros 'byor longs khoms med pa dag gis sgrub chen dang mi sbrel bar ci bder bskur na /
thog mar bka' brgyad bde 'dus kyi dbang chen dngos sta phyes te nyin gnyis la rdzogs pa bskur /
'di'ang sgrub chen gyi khog dbub sbyar nas zhag bdun lnga gsum gyis mtha' rten pa sngon tu grub na mchog tu 'gyur /
de nas smin lugs rdor sems kyis dbu bzung /
mjug dgongs 'dus pusti lung dbang grub kyi bar nyin re bzhin dbang rgyas bsdus dang bstun pa'i gang 'gro rim sgrub rim bskur bya /
de'ang zhi khro sgyu 'phrul /
rtsa gsum /
bla ma phyi sgrub skor pod gzhung thar chags las bsnon 'phri med cing /
bla ma nang sgrub chos dbang gsang 'dus dbang chen rjes su 'dod bum las 'byung ba'i zlum po bzhi dang gtor dbang bskur bas mtshon dkar chags ltar ma bu phan tshun mnyam sbrags kyis rdzogs par bya dgos te 'di nyid 'dod bum gyi rgyab chos lta bu yin pas so //
tshe sgrub gsang 'dus dbang rjes su bzhag nas gong smos ltar mthar dge byed pa legs so //
de ltar lag len rgyas bsdus gang byed kyang /
zhi khro
/bla ma zhi ba /
drag po /
'jam dpal sogs sde tshan re re'i mgor dngos sta phral nas zhag gis bar bcad ma bcad gang yang rung ba la dpung skud ku sha dngos su sbyin pa sogs phyag len rgyas pa'i phyogs grub na legs shing /
mi 'grub na dpung skud ku sha rnams dngos su mi sbyin nas 'grims pa smin gling sogs kyi phyag len yin zhing dngos sta zhag gis bar ma bcad na de dag dngos su sbyin pa la dgos pa cher med pas dbang rgyun tsam la khyad par med par go
/sde tshan so so'i dbur 'byung ba'i gtso che ba re'i sgrub mchod tshogs skong yang rgyas par grub na gal che zhing sgrub bskur re re bzhin las thabs med pa smos ma dgos /
dbang sgrub thams cad la'ang bsnyen bzlas brgya rtsa las mi nyung ba dang /
bum bzlas zur du dgos rigs la'ang de ltar bya /
gter srung sgos mchod yod rigs so so'i thad kar sbyar /
dmigs bsal med pa la dgong mor las byang rjes ma dang 'brel bar dam can spyi gtor gter gzhi bcas tshar re ma btang thabs med pas de kas 'thus par byed /
bdag 'jug re re bzhin mi lcogs pas ting 'dzin dbang len sogs dmigs bsal bshad pa rnams de kas 'thus shing /
spyi la rig pa'i me tog dor /
gang la'ang slong ma gzhug par gnang ba zhu ba ma chad pa gal che /
dbang phran /
rjes gnang /
srog gtad sogs zor yangs pa'i rigs rnams gsum bdun lnga sogs dus gcig la bsgrub bskur mnyam du byed pa rnying ma spyi'i lugs yin la don dang mi 'gal zhing sla bas de ltar bsham sgrub sogs bya /
chos skyong srog gtad rnams shin tu gnyan pas dam ldan gtor 'bul sogs ma chag pa byed mkhan ma gtogs khyab brdal du spel mi rung /
spyir drag sngags mngon spyod skor rnams dang /
rgyud bcu bdun gyi dbang /
khros ma'i gsang rgyud sogs ni rig 'dzin brgyud pa bar ma chad pa rnams kyis brgyud 'dzin dam ldan gcig gam gsum las mi spel ba phyag len gyi mtha' can yin pas dbang lung phal cher grub pa'i skabs sam yongs rdzogs grub pa'i rjes su de ltar spel mkhas su bya'o /
khrid thams cad so so'i dbang bskur grub pa'i rjes su bshad dgos pas rdor sems dang kar gling zhi khro lta bu'i dbang grub rjes mtshams sbyor bcas maN+Dal phul la khrid yig nyid dal bus go brda 'phrod par bklag nas dge bsngo sogs bya /
'di phyin chad kyi khrid rgyun yod tshad la des 'gre
/'di la bshad khrid dam khrid lung sgrags ma zer /
bshad mi shes mkhan nas nyab nyob mang po bshad na don 'bras med cing nyi ma 'phul /
bshad shes mkhan yin yang don rtsa khrid yig nang ma 'dus pa med cing rnam grangs mang po rdzogs thabs med pas 'di yis go chod par byed /
spyir kha bshad dpe klog gang byed kyang sgom don yid la nges shing go brda 'phrod pa khrid kyi mtshan nyid /
tshig don re re bzhin yid la zin mi dgos par sgra thos kyi shes 'jug bar ma chad pa tsam lung gi mtshan nyid yin pa chos spyan ldan pa'i bla ma dag bzhed pas de dag gi gnad kyang shes par bya dgos so //
las byang bsgrigs ma med rigs la skyabs sems bgegs gtor gyis mtshon pa'i sngon rjes yan lag sbyor 'os rnams las byang bde rol lta bu spyir smin lugs shig dang bstun na zor yangasabs legs shing /
bye brag gter kha lho byang dbus gsum /
khams lugs tha dad pa rnams so so'i rang lugs dang bstun shes na mchog tu 'gyur te /
dper na mchog gling zab bdun gyi rigs la sa bcad sde tshan gsang sngags spyi chings kyi skor la yod pa'i sngon 'gro dang mjug gi spyi chings sbyor dgos pas mtshon no //
bklag lung ni dbang gi bar bar du grub na'ang legs shing mi lcogs na dbang rnams grub zin pa'i rjes su dkyus gcig tu bklag pas chog go

/gnyis pa 'di'i skabs su nye bar mkho ba'i yo byad snga tshags su bya dgos pa ni /
dkyil 'khor sgo rdzogs yod pa rnams dang pad+ma chos 'byung sogs maN+Dal rigs kyi ras bris /
tsaka li tshang ba bcas med thabs med pas de dag tshogs pa gzhir byas /
rgyud dang gzhung pod kyi glegs bam so so la mkho ba 'dzom na rab /
ma 'dzom na rgyud gsang snying tsam dang so so'i sgrub thabs kyi yi ge dar gyis dril ba /
btags grol 'khor lo dang glegs bam /
mthong grol klong snying rig 'dzin srog 'khor /
tshe 'khor dang srung 'khor spyi 'gro
/gdugs dkar 'khor lo /
chos skyong rnams dang rnam sras dzam dmar sogs kyi srog 'khor bla rdo /
sde brgyad bla rdo so so yod dgos kyang ma 'dzom na /
mgon po spyi la gri snying bsres pa'i snying gzugs tshon btang ba'i nang du sgrub khang byang ngos nas rdo nag gru gsum lag pa ma reg pa gri lcags gri gug gam gri rtses blangs pa la hU~M bris pa dang /
bka' rgya mar bkod pa'i mgon po spyi'i srog 'khor bcas dar mthing nag gis dril nas gri lcags ga'u zur gsum du btsud pa /
lha mo spyi la mtsho rdel sngon po lag pas ma reg cing gnam gyis ma mthong bar blangs pa la b+h+yo bris pa dang ma mo spyi'i srog 'khor dar gyis btums pa /
chos skyong sde brgyad spyi la pha waM long bur mtshal gyis tri bris pa rnams dang /
rdzas cha'i rigs /
byang gter thugs sgrub kyi gtum mo'i me dbang dang sku gsum rigs 'dus kyi tsha rdzas grang rdzas /

/gsum pa bye brag so so'i gshom bkod bshad pa la'ang /
thog mar dbang bskur tshugs nye ba'i nyin snga ma rnams su bka' brgyad rdor sems kyis mtshon pa'i gtor ma 'og tu dgos pa rnams las thog mar mkho ba rnams dang /
spyi 'gre chog pa /
bla gtor ram zhi gtor /
dpal gtor rigs gnyis /
zur gsum dmar po rgyan ldan sogs lnga bdun re tsam /
tshe 'brang shing lo dang nyi zla'i kha rgyan can kha shas rnams mar zan gyis bcos te tshon dang rgyan spros spus legs bya /
rtsa gsum spyi dang khyad par chos srung gter srung rnams re re bzhin 'phral 'phral gshom pa ma lcogs na /
bla ma yi dam mkha' 'gro
/chos skyong dngos grub rol mtsho rjes 'brang dang bcas pa'i gtor ma legs par bzhengs /
las byang la dgos pa'i mchod gtor rigs tshang bar bca'o //
dngos gzhi tshugs pa'i thog mar gnas khang phyags dar bya /
rtsa ba gsum gyi sku gsung thugs kyi rten byin rlabs can rnams dang /
chos skyong gi rten sogs bkram /
bla bre dar 'phan sogs rgyan gyi bkod pas mdzes par bya /
sgrub chen dang sbrel na sngon 'gro sa chog phyi nang mtshams gcod nas bzung /
rjes kyi bya ba rnams grub kyi bar lag len de'i lugs bya dgos kyang 'dir yi ges 'jigs pas ma spros la /
skabs der ni dkyil 'khor lding khri brtsegs mar byas pa'i 'og tu rdor sems dkyil 'khor rgyun bzhag gi mtha' skor du phyi nang mchod pa brgya rtsa sogs bsgrig
/steng mar skabs so so'i dkyil 'khor dbang rdzas rnams res mos su bsham /
sgab bskor sogs kyi chas rnams spyi ltar bya ba yin no //
sgrub chen dang ma 'brel na stegs bu rgya che ba khebs bzang pos bkab cing /
dbang mang po sbrel skabs dkyil 'khor dang dbang rdzas rnams shong nges pa'i zur bzhir rgyal mtshan /
logs bzhir 'phan gzug
/steng du bla bre dar dpyangs kyis mdzes par brgyan /
de steng dkyil 'khor gang yin bkram pa'i dbus su bum gtor brtsegs mar 'god dgos pa'i rigs la 'phrul stegs rim pa gnyis pa blang bzhag bde ba dang /
bum gtor gang rung 'jog dgos pa spyi dang sku tshab bzhugs gdan sogs rkang gsum 'jog dgos pas de'ang grangs ka mang du bsdogs /
gal te dkyil 'khor ras bris mi 'dzoms pa'i dbang byin rlabs chung ngu'i rigs la maN+Dal steng tshom bu lha grangs bkod kyang chog mod /
tshom bu'ang tshon gyis kha bsgyur ba'i 'bras la mar gyi snying po byas te lha mdog dang mtshungs pa'i che chung mang po grub na legs /
bum pa la gsar ma'i lugs su gos bzang po dang srad bu sogs kyis dkri ba las dmigs su ma gsungs kyang /
rnying ma gter ma'i phyogs phal mo cher mgul chings dmigs bsal du bshad cing da lta phyag len du'ang mdzad pas /
dmigs su ma bshad pa rnams la'ang mgul chings lha gtso bo'i sku mdog dang mthun par bcings /
bum rdzas kyang spyi khyab thams cad bla med kho na yin pas so lnga 'ba' zhig dang dri bzang gi chu sbyar /
tshe dbang phal cher dang /
'jam dbyangs lta bu dmigs bsal can la nyer lnga 'debs /
byin rlabs kyi rigs sogs kyi thod pa'i bdud rtsi chang dang bdud rtsi chos sman sbyar /
rig tsaka yod pa'i dbang bzhi'i rigs rnams la de steng mngar gsum ro bro nges par bya /

dur khrod chas rnams bkod /

/stag sham rdo rje drag rtsal dbang chen la /
dkyil 'khor ras bris sam tshom bu lha grangs steng many+dzi la bum pa mgul chings sngon po kha rgyan gseb gtso bo'i sku tsaka can /
mdun phyogs thod phreng sde lnga sogs lha tsaka tshang ba /

/thod pa'am rak+sha'i phreng ba /

/'char ka gnam skas ma'i zor dbang la /

thod khrag
/bdud rtsi /

'byor pas ma bde na bum gtor brtsegs /

/gtor ma rgyas pa lcogs dka' bas dmar gtor zur gsum 'khor drug dang thebs kyu mang pos bskor ba dar gdugs dbub /

/zor kong dkyus ma gcig

/sgrub thabs glegs bam /

gtor dbang /

mdun du dmar gtor thebs kyu mang pos bskor ba bsham /

/thugs mchog rdo rje'i nA ga rak+sha la /

mdun du 'bul gtor dkar gtor cha lnga bsham /

thugs rdor nA ga rak+sha la /
drag dkyil gzhung mthun ras bris bkram pa'am /

me hom rnams kyang 'du bya'o //

//de nas pad+ma gsung gi zhi sgrub kyi dang po tshe sgrub kyi skor las /
lung lugs tshe sgrub la /
ras bris steng rkang gsum la bum pa snying po lnga'i bcud kyis bkang ba'i khar tshe 'brang rgya gram nyi zlas mtshan pa /
rgyab tu tshe mda' me long /
g.yas g.yon tshe ril tshe chang /
zhabs bsil bzhi bsnol gyis mtha' bskor /

nyang gter mtsho skyes rdo rje la /
ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor ram ma 'dzom na maN+Dal la 'bru dkar gyi tshom bu lha grangs bkod pa'i dbus su many+dzi la rin po che'i bum pa chas bcud ldan pa'i khar thod pa bdud rtsis gang bar gzhung gsal tshe rdzas sum cu'i ril bu btab pa'i khar /
me long la sin+d+hu ras chos 'byung nyis brtsegs kyi dbus su hrIHla rtsa sngags dang badzra gu rus bskor ba dang chos 'byung gi zur drug la g.yung drung re bris pas bkab pa'i steng du dar dmar po'i gur phub pa la gzungs thag rdo rje btags pa dang /

de steng bum pa pad+mas bskor ba'i khar rin po ches brgyan pa /
ri rab mtha' skor pad+ma phyi nang sbrags ma yod rgyan spros can bsham /
mdun du thod chang khar me long dang shel rdo bzhag
!
yongs rdzogs gtad rgya'i dbang la /
dkyil 'khor dbus su many+dzi'i khar rnam bum /
kha rgyan la rab gtso 'khor yongs 'dzugs dang /
ma 'dzom na bla ma dang 'phags pa'i sku tsaka bzhugs /
g.yas su bla ma'i gtor ma rin chen zur drug dang /
'phags pa'i gtor ma pad phreng bum dbyibs /
dpal mgon gtor ma dpal gtor la bshos bu brgyad kyis bskor ba sku tsag gis brgyan pa /
g.yon du thod chang dam rdzas sbyar ba'i khar me long la sin+d+hu ra'i dkyil 'khor pad+ma 'dab brgyad /
dbus su hrIHma /
mtha' skor du rtsa sngags dang dbyangs gsal gyis bskor bas bkab la dar dmar gyis g.yogs pa'i steng shel rdo bzhag
/mdun du sgrub dpe phreng ba rdor dril rnams rin po che'i snod 'brus gang ba'i nang du bzhag
/rgyab tu bka' srung bye brag pa'i gtor ma gong smros sku tsag gis brgyan pa rnams snod gcig tu bzhag go
!
/grol tig pad+ma'i dbang phyug la /
tshom bu gcig gi khar bum thod me long shel rdo rnams brtsegs /
!

bdud 'dul nam mkha' rgyal po la /
sta gon rdzas bzhi /

/rgya can 'jig rten dbang phyug la /

gar dbang zla rgyal gyi rtsa gsum snying thig la /

/phyogs gang bder gsang dbang thod pa'i bdud rtsi /

me long gsal ba /
gtso mo'i sku tsaka
/mda' gzhu /
mar me /
rig tsaka rnams dang rjes gnang chas /
phreng ba /
dung /
glegs bam /
dur khrod chas brgyad /
sha lnga bdud rtsi lnga'i ril bu thod chang du blugs pa'am ma 'dzom na gzugs brnyan bris pa bcas bkod /
bka' srung bka' gtad la gtor ma zur gsum gtso 'khor gsum pa dar gdugs can yang bkod /
!
gtor dbang la gtor ma gzhung gsal sku tsaka dar gdugs kyis brgyan pa dkyil 'khor kyi dbus su bkod /
snga ma'i zhar byung byed na dkyil 'khor rgyab phyogs lta bur bzhag
/gnyis ka la'ang slob ma la sbyin rgyu zas sna dang thod chang lhan cig tu bkod do /
!
/rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i tshe sgrub sogs bzhi la /
'dzom na ras bris dkyil 'khor /
ma 'dzom na mkha' 'gro bzhi la rim bzhin tshom bu lha mdog bkod pa'i steng so so'i dbang rdzas bsham dgos pas /
'di la tshom bu dkar po gcig
/de steng tshe 'brang /
g.yas g.yon du tshe ril chang dang mda' dar bkod /
!
rin chen mkha' 'gro'i nor sgrub la /
gtor ma rin chen 'bar ba'i dbyibs can nor bu mig gsum mang pos mdzes par bskor ba rgyan spros dar gdugs ser po can /
g.yas su thod pa'i bdud rtsi /
g.yon du thod pa mtshan ldan 'khor lo gzhung gsal dang g.yang rdzas sna tshogs pas bkang ba bzhag
!
/pad+ma mkha' 'gro'i dbang sdud la /
sku rten bris sku /
gsung rten srog 'khor /
thugs rten b+han+d+har dbang gi ril bus bkang ba rnams gzhung mthun byas la g.yas g.yon mdun gsum du bkod /
dbang gi me thab /
yam shing /
mar khu /
mngar gsum la rdzas sbyar gyi ril bu /
me tog dmar po chang gis sbags pa /
lan tshwa bcas sreg rdzas rnams dang /
dgang blugs /
gser skyems mchod pa bcas 'du bya /
!
las kyi mkha' 'gro'i zor dbang la /
zangs lcags kyi snod du zor gtor khro mo'i zhal can gtor chung lha grangs kyis bskor ba /
de rgyab zor kong /
zur gsum brgyad la /
shar du yungs kar /
lhor rtsang /
nub tu dug
/byang du rdo /
shar lhor me /
lho nub dug khrag
/nub byang mda'/

mtshe nyungs sha khrag gis brgyan cing dar nag gi gdugs phub la /
g.yas g.yon du sngags byang dang /
gnam lcags rdo rje bzhag
/phyag rgya bzhi'i chas /
hom dang ling+ga /

/thod ngan du khrag thun sbyar ba rnams nye bar bsdog go

/g.yag char sngon mo'i sgrol ljang la /
maN+Dal tshom bu ljang gu gcig bkod pa'i steng many+dzi la bum pa nyer lnga'i rdzas dang chings ljang can /
mdun du dbang gtor dkar zlum /
sku tsaka
/sngags phreng /
ut+pal ljang gu'i tsaka li bcas bkod /
!
bla ma dgongs 'dus mkha' 'gro'i dbang /
ras bris steng rnam bum thod chang me long chos 'byung bsnol ma'i dbus su pad+ma 'dab bzhi'i lte bar hrIHma baM/
'dab bzhir ha ri ni sa /
rtsibs drug dga' 'khyil bris pa rnams brtsegs pa dar dmar gyis bkab /
rigs lnga'i phyag mtshan so so ba /
dbu rgyan /
me long /
mkha' 'gro'i sku rten /
sgrub yig dbang phreng /
cod pan rnams dang /
rgyab tu mkha' 'gro'i gtor ma gtso 'khor lnga rgyan can bkod /
!
rat+na'i mtsho rgyal skor gsum gyi mtsho rgyal la /
ras bris steng gtor gdan phor pa lta bu'i steng pad+ma 'dab brgyad /
de steng rin chen 'bar ba 'dab brgyad ril bus bskor ba rgyan spros sku tsaka dar gdugs can bzhag
!
sgrol ma la /
maN+Dal tshom bu gcig bkod pa'i steng bum pa nyer lnga'i rdzas dang rgyan ldan /
!
khros nag la /
ras bris steng rnam bum thod chang me long chos 'byung lte bar ma /
mtha' skor snying po bris pa bzhag la dar dmar gyis bkab pa'i steng du khros nag sku brnyan bris 'bur gang rigs bzhugs /
'di gsum dkyus gcig tu bskur na /
g.yas g.yon dbus gsum du bkod /
!
phag mo zab rgya la /
ras bris dbus thod chang byang sems dkar dmar chos sman btab pa'i khri'u la dpal gtor rta zhal dang phag zhal gyis mtshan pa rgyan spros dar gdugs can bsham /
!
phag dkar ye shes 'khor lo la /
sku mtshan ma'i dkyil 'khor gzhung mthun bris pa'am /
maN+Dal la me tog dkar po'i tshom bu gcig bkod pa'i steng khri'u la gsung bdud rtsi'i dkyil 'khor ka pA la a mr-ita'i bcud ldan gyi khar /
thugs me long la sin+d+hu ra brdal bar chos 'byung bsnol ma'i dbus su hrIHgra bzhir dga' 'khyil re re bris pas dgab /
mdun du sku tsaka
/shel phreng /
kha T+wAM ga
/sgrub yig
/sna tshogs rdo rje dang bdud rtsi /
g.yas su thod pa mtshan ldan gzhung mthun tshe ril gyis bkang ba'i kha dar dmar gyis bkab pa dang tshe 'brang dkar mngar bza' btung /
g.yon du bdud rtsi ril bus bkang ba'i sman gyi pho brang /
skong chog dbang rten mar me rnams bkod /
!
zhig gling sgrol dkar la /
rdul tshon sogs kyi dkyil 'khor steng rnam bum nyer lnga'i bcud ldan kha rgyan la sku tsaka btsugs pa'i mdun du dkar zlum rgyan ldan /
shel rdo /
ut+pal dkar po rnams dang /
ril chang mda' dar spyi ltar /
shel phreng /

!
/sprul sku'i snying thig gi sgrol dkar la /

g.yon du shel rdo dang /
shel phreng /
rgyab tu ril chang sna bdun rdzas brgyad phyogs bsdus bcas /

srog sgrub phag mo la /
ras bris dbus rnam bum bkod pa'i 'og tu mar me sbar /
mdun sogs su gsang thod me long sin+d+hu ra'i thig le can dar dmar gyis bkab /
me long g.ya' dag shel rdo /
rma bya'i mdongs /

bdud rtsi /

smin gling gsang ye la /
dkyil 'khor gzhung mthun steng rnam bum thod chang me long chos 'byung lte bar hrIH
zur gsum du oM AHhU~M/

bgegs gtor dpal 'bar btsugs pa dang /
slob ma'i gdan dga' 'khyil dmar ser yang 'du bya /
!
stag sham mtsho rgyal la /
ras bris sam maN+Dal steng tshom bu gtso 'khor dgu de rgyab phyogs bzhir bkod pa'i steng /
 gtor ma rgya gar dam gzugs ma'am ma shes na gtor zlum dkar po pad 'dab bzhi pa'i phyogs bzhir dkar bshos bzhi /

/chos gling khros nag la /
bsnyen sgrub bcas 'dzom dka' bas dbang bskur dkyus mar spyi 'gro tsam du /

de steng thod pa'i bdud rtsi dang me long shel rdo bkod /
tshe ril chang mda' dar bcas bsham /
!
klong snying yum bka' bde chen rgyal mo'i rtsa dbang la /
ras bris sam tshom bu dmar po gcig bkod pa'i steng thod chang nyer lnga'i rdzas dang chos sman gyis bkang ba'i khar sin+d+hu ra'i me long chos 'byung bsnol ma bris pa'i dbus su dga' 'khyil tAM gyis mtshan pa /

!

/gter gsar zab bdun legs ldan la /

de rgyab bzhi bris pas bkab pa'i steng shel rdo bzhag

ral gri

/gur mgon srog gi spu gri la /

/zab mo skor dgu'i phyi sgrub gtor dbang thun mong ba la /
maN+Dal dkyil 'khor ram me tog nag po'i tshom bu lnga bkod pa'i steng du khri'u'i khar lcags sam thod snod du dpal gtor dmar po gtso 'khor lnga mtheb kyus bskor ba la sku tsaka dang dar gdugs kyis brgyan pa bkod /
'di la bsdu na sngags byang phyag mtshan mi dgos /

dpal mgon ma ning la /
maN+Dal gru gsum mthing nag gi dbus 'bru nag khrag gis sbags pa'i tshom bu dbus su che chung gsum /
de rgyab lnga bkod pa'i steng du dbang gtor /
g.yas su rnam bum dang gtso sku /
mdun nas g.yas bskor du stag zhon sku dang ber nag
/bing sku dang sgrub pod srog snying /

trak+shad sku dang seng ldeng phur pa khro zhal can rnams bkod /

/trak+shad dwags po lugs la /

/mtheb kyu bcu gnyis kyis bskor /

!
shwa na'i zhal can la /

/de mdun chung ba gcig

!
byang gter bstan srung yongs rdzogs la /

oM shrI ma hA ka la ga Na gu ti yo gi shwa ri sa ma ya hU~M dzaHdzaH

/tshogs bdag gter ma khams byon ma la /
ras bris steng rnam bum /
shar du gtor ma sku tsaka can /
lhor gri snying srog 'khor can /
nub tu thod chang /
byang du brub khung nya'o phur bu mtshon cha thun rdzas /
dbus su lha tsaka rgyab tu sngags byang bris pa rnams dang /
sgrub yig bkod /
!
gter gsar shwa na'i gtor dbang la /
tshom bu'i steng dbang gtor thod snod du dmar gtor thog mdel dbyibs can /
gtor chung nyer bzhi dang mtheb kyu mang pos bskor ba /
me ri dang ral gri thod khrag gis brgyan pa la /
mda' dar nag po me long sku rten bcas bkod /
sngags byang /
ral gri thod khrag
/g.yas g.yon sman raka bkod /
!
gter gsar chos skyong dgongs 'dus snying po la /
ras bris sam tshom bu lha grangs dbus dbang gtor dang sku tsaka
/sngags byang /
phyag mtshan gri thod bcas /
!
zhig gling ma hA kA la dpal mgon bdun cu'i srog gtad la /
dkyil 'khor dbus khri'u la zangs lcags kyi snod du gtor ma ri rab bang rim bzhi pa'i steng gru gsum gdan thabs /
de steng mgon po'i dpal gtor dang lha mo'i gtor ma bzhag
/bang rim rnams su lha brgyad /
klu brgyad /
gza' brgyad /
phyogs skyong bcu /
rgyal chen bzhi /
'jigs byed dgu
/rgyu skar nyer brgyad rnams so so'i dbyibs mthun gyi gtor ma bkod /
mi shes na bshos zlum grangs tshang bkod pa la rgyan spros dar gdugs can dang /
thod phreng bzhag
!
/e ka dzA Ti sde bdun la /
ras bris sam maN+Dal gru gsum bsnol mar tshom bu bdun gyi khar many+dzi la dbus dang phyogs bzhi /
byang shar du gnyis bcas sde bdun so so'i gtor ma sku rten mda' dar bcas pa bkod pa'i mdun du mchod gtor spyi spungs sman raka bcas /
lhor ri rab bang rim bzhi pa'i steng gi dbus dang phyogs bzhir mar me lnga bzhag pa /
nub tu rten rdzas dang bcas pa'i mda' dar /
byang du b+han+d+ha dam rdzas kyis bkang ba rnams dang /

gu gul tshil chen sogs kyi spos bcas /

rat+na lugs kyi rjes gnang la /
ras bris sam 'bru nag tshom bu gcig pa'i steng du dbang gtor sku rten bcas pa'i mdun du mchod gtor dang bdud rtsi bsham /
!
smin lugs la /
de dang 'dra ba'i steng /
sngags byang /
yod na bla rdo srog 'khor /
med na phyag mtshan snying dang zhing dbyug dam rdzas bcas /
!
re ti rang byung rgyal mo la /
ras bris steng dbang gtor rgyan ldan bkod /
phreng ba bzhag
!
/nyang gter rdo rje gshog rgod ma la /
ras bris sam tshom bu'i steng dbang gtor rgyan ldan bkod /
!
grol tig gshog rgod ma de dang 'dra ba'i thog
/mdun du phyag mtshan lcags kyu rdo rje dgra satwa thod pa rnams /
g.yas su tshogs rdzas /
rgyab tu rten rdzas /
mda' mo dung shwa can /
g.yon du srog yig b+h+yo dang sngags byang rnams bkod /
yi dam dpal gtor zhabs su lha mo'i bla rdo spyi mthun nam ma 'dzom na mtsho rdel sngon po la b+h+yo yig bris pa dar sngon gyis btum pa bzhag
/re ba tshon skud dum thod pa rnams dang /
thod rnga rkang gling sman raka gtor ma rnams phyogs bsdus gtad chog bzhag
!
/gnam chos a phyi la /
gzungs dbang ltar bkod /
!
g.yu sgron ma'i bka' gtad la /
'bru sil ma bkram pa'i dbus so so'i gtor ma /

/nas theb gang /
phyag mtshan bcas bkod /

/rdo rje rab brtan ma'i thun mong rjes gnang la /
maN+Dal dang sgrub gtor gzhung mthun /
sku tsaka
/ral gri ne'u le'i gzugs bkod /
!
srog sgrub ma la /
ras bris steng dbus su gtso mo /
g.yas g.yon mdun gsum du 'khor gyi gtor ma so sor bkod /
!
gza' bdud la /
ras bris dbus su bum pa rgyan ldan /
mdun du dbang gtor sman raka dang bcas pa /
lhor chu srin rgyal mtshan sbrul zhags mda' gzhu me phung rnams so so ba /
byang du 'khor gza' brgyad kyi sku gzugs dang phyag mtshan gyi tsaka li phyogs bsdus gnyis bcas bkod /
'bul gtor nub tu'o /
!
/shan pa dmar nag la /
ras bris steng dbang gtor la mda' dar khyad par ba btsugs pa /
phyogs bzhir ral gri
/gri gug
/snying zhags /
thod khrag bzhi /
mtshams bzhir skam rlon gyi thun snod /
zor gtor gru gsum /
me hom gyi ting lo gru gsum /
mnan pa'i sAts+tsha rnams bzhag
/mdun mchod g.yas g.yon du zhing lpags glang ko stag sham so so ba /
g.yon du 'brang rgyas bza' btung bcas bkod /
!
rat+na lugs kyi rjes gnang la /
maN+Dal steng sgrub gtor sku rten dar gdugs dmar po bcas gzhung mthun /
g.yas su ral gri gri gug
/g.yon du snying zhags ban+d+ha /
mdun du mchod gtor rnams bsham /
!
pu tra ming sring la /
gong du mgon po'i mchod gtor mtho bar bsham /
de mdun ming sring la rtag gtor zur brgyad kyi mdun 'bul gtor bcas bsham /
!
dkar bdud lcam dral la /
maN+Dal chos 'byung gru gsum dkar po'i dbus su 'bru dkar po'i tshom bu bkod pa'i steng du 'brang rgyas dkar po phug ron gyi gzugs dang bcas pa bkod /
de'i g.yas su chos 'byung gru gsum nag po la 'bru nag gi tshom bu'i khar dmar gtor gru gsum bkod /
!
las gshin la /
maN+Dal mthing nag gru gsum thod ra me ris bskor ba la tshom bu che chung gnyis /
de rgyab brgyad bkod pa'i steng du gtor ma rgyan ldan bkod /
!
dam can mgar dmar rjes gnang la /

g.yas su bla rdo dang sgrub yig
/g.yon du rdo rje dang snying gzugs bzhag go

/'gro 'dul las 'phro gling pa'i dam can la /

zla gam gsum la dmar gtor /

/byang du mdung dmar tho ba /

me long dang mda' dar bzhag

/zhing skyong seng gdong la /

mdun du sku tsaka

zan ling gnyis shog ling gcig hom du bkod pa bcas /

bdud 'dul lugs kyi zhing skyong la /

rgyab tu mda' dar bla rdo srog 'khor btags pa bzhag
!
/srog sgrub drag po sde bzhi'i bka' gtad la /
ras bris steng rnam bum chas ldan /
phyogs bzhi drag po sde bzhi'i gtor ma dar gdugs sku tsaka sogs rgyan ldan /
mdun du shel rdo me long hU~M yig sgro mdongs /
g.yas su gzhung pod bgrang phreng thod chang /
rgyab tu thod khrag
/g.yon du brub khung nya'o /
gdab phur phyag rgya bzhi sgrol gri rnams dang /
gzhan yang thal raka zhag gsum /
dur khrod chas /
phyag mtshan gri gug sbrul zhags lcags kyu be con zhing dbyug rgyu zhags tho ba sbud pa rnams kyi tsaka li dang /
rak+sha'i phreng ba bcas bkod /
!
zhing skyong dur khrod ma mo la /
sin+d+hu ra'i dkyil 'khor gzhung gsal steng rten gtor rgyan ldan /
mdun du mar zan 'bul gtor ra dkar mo'i 'o ma la sogs bkod /
gla rtsi spos dkar dang sbyar ba'i spos kyang bsdog

/sha za kha mo che'i srog gtad la /

bgrang phreng bcas bkod /

brtan ma bcu gnyis la /
ras dkar po'i gzhi la pad+ma 'dab ma bcu gnyis mu khyud dang bcas pa'am tshom bu lha grangs kyi dbus su gong gnon bla ma yi dam gang rung bkod dgos pas skabs 'dir bla ma'i gtor ma bzhag
/pad 'dab bcu gnyis la brtan ma'i gtor ma sku tsaka dar 'phan bcas /
shar stod nas brtsams te g.yas bskor du 'god /
sman raka gtor gsum /
dkar mngar phud skyems phye mar sogs sger mchod gzhung gsal /
bzang shing spos dkar sogs 'du bya /
!
pe har srog gtad la /

'di yan gyi chos skyong thams cad la mdun du mchod gtor gtso 'khor lha grangs dang mtshungs pa'i g.yas g.yon sman raka 'god dgos pa ni thams cad la shes par bya'o //

//de nas dgos dbang khyad par can gyis bzhag pa'i rdo rje g.yung drung gling pa'i yab sras bcud dril la /
gzhung gsal dkyil 'khor ram /
ma 'dzom na maN+Dal tshom bu gcig bkod pa'i steng /

bon gter kun grol las 'phro gling pa'i mkha' 'gro gsang mdzod kyi dbang la /

//las bye brag pa'i thog ma srung ba'i skor las /
rgya phur bu'i dug khrag rdzas srung gi byin rlabs la /
'dzom na dug khrag rwa srung tshad ldan byas pa dgos kyang dkyus su 'dzom dka' bas rdzas rgod sogs sbyar nas bsgrubs pa'i rwa srung stegs bur bkod /

gnam chos 'jigs med rdo rje dang /
rdo rje mchu la gzungs dbang gi chas so /

/zhig gling dmag zlog nyer lnga'i rgyal chen sde bzhi'i bka' gtad la /
ras bris dbus su rgyal chen sde bzhi'i gtor ma rin po che'i snod bzhi so so'i nang rim bzhin ri rab bang rim bzhi brtsegs re re bkod la de steng shar du lha bshos dbyibs pad 'dab mang pos bskor ba /
lhor gru bzhi mkhar thabs rtser ral gris brgyan pa /
nub tu zlum po 'dab bzhi rtse mor sbrul rigs lngas dkris pa /
byang du khang bzang sum brtsegs /
de bzhi'i rtse mor so so'i sku rten rang mdog mda' dar dang bcas pa /
ri rab rtse mor rgyal mtshan btsugs pa bzhag
/de steng khri'ur rnam bum chings sngon can /

dug srung byang gter dug dbang rdo rje pha lam gyi dbang gi bcas bsham sngags 'chang dbang po'i sde'i gsung las 'byung ba ltar bya dgos /[ \u0fcb ]dug dbang rdo rje pha lam gyi bcas bsham /
gnas dben par slob dpon kha lhor bltas pa'i mdun du ras dkar kha tshar ma nyams pa gru bzhir bltabs pa'i steng du /
dkyil 'khor chos 'byung gru gsum pa'i dbyibs can /
de yang gsum gnyis nas dkar dang cha gcig sran ma nag po las byas pa'i lhor kha bstan pa'i dbus man dzi'i khar bum pa 'o mar bcas pa'i dri bzang gis phyed gang ba'i steng du /
rin po che'i snod du /
gser thig po dang sman chen rma bya'i mdongs /
zur gsum lho rtser gu lang nag po lcags kyi rwa co 'phyar ba /
nub byang rtse la shrI ral pa can mda' gzhu 'geng pa /
byang shar rtse mor dbang phyug chen po tri shU la 'geng pa /
gsum ka yang gcer bu ling+ga gyen du bsgreng ba nyams dod par 'bur du grub pa /
bum par zhal bstan pa'i chos 'byung gi leb gsum gyi shar du lug nag 'og can gyi rkang pa g.yas pa'i dpyi lhu /
byang du bar lhu /
nub tog rtse lta bu /
gsum ka yang sha nang gyen bstan gyi bcad kha phyir bstan pa /
slob dpon gyi mdun g.yas su /
nub ngos nas tshur zlum gtor gsum dang sher dbang gi rdzas chu gtsang la cu gang dang li khri btab pa /
bzhi pa'i rten chos 'byung gtor ma zhes pa ste /
de yang 'og nas rim par zhi rgyas dbang drag gi dbyibs kha dog so sor bsgyur ba las /
steng gi drag po thog gi mde'u lta bu ste /
gtor ma bzhi ka yang dkar dmar gyis brgyan /
mtha' skor mchod pa g.yon bskor bkod pa'i shar du sha sna sogs bza' bca' gang yang rung ba'i tshogs gang 'dzom mngon par 'du bya'o /[ \u0fcb ]!
/gnam chos dgongs gter 'od zer can ma la /
maN+Dal tshom bu gcig bkod pa'i dbus bum pa nyer lnga'i rdzas ldan mgul chings dkar po kha rgyan ldan pa dang /
mdun rgyab gang bder dbang gtor sku tsaka dar gdugs kyis brgyan pa /
rtags brgyad tsaka li bcas bzhag go /
!
//de nas zhi ba'i las tshogs kyi /
thog mar bgegs dang bar chad zhi ba'i skor la /
chos gling bar chad sel ba'i rnam 'joms bum chog la /
pad+ma 'dab brgyad steng bum pa rdzas gzhung gsal lam ma 'dzom na nyer lnga'i bcud ldan bkod /
!
mchog gling thugs sgrub rak+sha thod phreng la /
maN+Dal tshom bu dbus su gcig 'khor bcus bskor ba'i steng rnam bum /
mdun du dpal gtor /
sku tsaka
/sngags byang ngam thod phreng /
phyag mtshan rdo rje thod pa'i tsaka li bcas /
!
thugs sgrub mi g.yo ba rigs bzhi ka la /
maN+Dal pad+ma 'dab brgyad rdo rwa me ri'i bskor ba'i lte ba rang mdog la tshom bu de mtshungs sam phyag mtshan bris pa'i steng du rnam bum /
sku tsaka
/ral gri zhags pa sogs phyag mtshan so so /
mdun du dbang gtor bcas /
!
zhi byed spyi bsdus lha btsun sngon mo'i zhi byed skor bdun la /
maN+Dal pad+ma 'dab brgyad tshom bu dkar po can gyi steng du bum pa chings dkar nyer lnga'i bcud ldan /
mdun rgyab gang bder zlum gtor dar gdugs dkar pos spras pa /
so so'i sku tsaka dang /
phyag mtshan /
shel phreng /
dar dang rin po che'i rgyan /
rdzas brgyad bcas /

so so'i mtha' rten chas /

dbyangs can ma dkar mo la /
gur gum gla rtsi gi waM tsan dan dkar po bzhi cha mnyam du sbyar ba stegs bu la 'thor ba'i maN+Dal la ba'i 'o mar sbrang rtsi bzhi mnyam rnams sbyar bas pad+ma 'dab brgyad dbus su hrIM dang 'dab brgyad la a A sogs dbyangs bcu drug gnyis re bkod pa bzhag
/de steng dkar gsum mngar gsum bzhi mnyam rnams sbyar ba'i zan gyis ting lo ba mar sbrang rtsis bkang ba'i mar me slob ma'i grangs mnyam bkod /
mdun du zlum gtor che chung gnyis chang bu bcas bzhag go
!
/bla ma smra ba'i seng ge la /
ras bris sam tshom bu lha grangs steng rnam bum chings dkar /
mdun du lha tsaka
/g.yas g.yon du sngags phreng dang shes rab ril bu /
rgyab tu dbang gtor bcas /
!
klong gsal phag dkar shes rab gsal byed la /
dkyil 'khor chos 'byung gzhung gsal lam /
tshom bu'i steng bum pa chings dkar /
mtha' skor du shel phreng /
thod chang /
dril bu /
shes rab ril bu rang gzhung nas bshad pa ltar dang /
zlum gtor dkar po rgyan bcas /
!
kun mkhyen bla ma'i dgongs gter phag dkar shes rab gsal byed la /
rdul tshon nam ras bris kyi maN+Dal steng many+dzi la rnam bum bkod pa'i khar thod pa bdud rtsis bkang ba la /
sin+d+hu ra'i me long chos 'byung baM yig sngags phreng gis brgyan pas bkab pa'o //
!
//bsod nams longs spyod rgyas par byed pa la /
rnam sras phyi sgrub ser chen la /
ras bris sam sna tshogs pad+ma 'dab brgyad steng rten gtor khang brtsegs ma bkod /
de'i g.yas su bum gdan pad+ma 'dab bzhi 'am tshom bu'i khar bum pa bcud ldan /
g.yon du mchod gtor zlum po gtso 'khor dgu pa /
mdun du dbu rgyan /
rgyal mtshan dang ne'u'i tsaka li bkod /
!
nang sgrub mdung dmar can la /
ras bris sam pad+ma 'dab brgyad dmar po'i steng rten gtor sku rten bcas /
shar du spos dang dri chab kyi dung zhal /
shar lhor mar me /
lhor dngul snod du chang phud /
lho nub tu mda' dar /
nub tu 'bru sna'i me tog
/nub byang du mdung dmar /
byang du 'bul gtor sha sogs kyis brgyan pa /
byang shar du dmar gtor rnams bsham /
gnam lcags rdo rje rgyab ngos la bzhag
!
/gsang sgrub drag po rta sngon la /
ras bris khar rten gtor sku rten can /
lcags kyi rdo rje sngar ltar dang /
ral gri'ang bzhag
!
/yang gsang phyag mtshan bzhi pa'i rjes gnang bsham bkod nang sgrub mdung dmar can dang 'dra /
!
rat+na'i mdung dmar la /
ras bris sam tshom bu dmar po gtso 'khor lnga pa'i steng rten gtor sku tsaka bcas /
g.yas su mdung dmar rgyal mtshan /
g.yon du ne le lcags kyu /
rgyab tu gri snying bla rdo dang sgrub yig
/mdun du tshe 'brang dang 'brang rgyas zhal dkar bza' btung zas sna bsham /
!
pad gling lugs kyi mdung dmar can la /
ras bris sam stegs dmar por me tog dmar po'i tshom bu gtso 'khor dgu bkod pa'i dbus su rten gtor sku rten can /
g.yas g.yon du mdung dmar rgyal mtshan ne'u le lcags kyu /
mdun du gri snying bul tog
/sgrub yig
/rgyab tu tshe 'brang bza' btung bcas /
!
byang gter nor lha yongs rdzogs la /
dkyil 'khor ram tshom bu gtso 'khor lnga /
de rgyab brgyad /
mdun mtshams g.yas g.yon du gnyis /
de rgyab bzhi bkod pa'i steng du bum pa chings nag can /
g.yas su dzaM gtor rin chen 'bar ba /
g.yon du thod chang mngar gsum sbyar ba /
rgyab phyogs zangs snod du dzaM nag gi sku dang chu sbyin chas bsham /
!
zhang blon la /
pad+ma 'dab brgyad dam tshom bu'i khar rten gtor sku tsaka can bkod /
!
grwa mngon dzaM dmar la /
pad+ma 'dab brgyad dmar po'i steng khri'ur thod chang bu ram bdud rtsi ril bu btab pa /
de mdun gtor ma rin chen 'bar ba'i dbyibs can zas snas brgyan pa bkod /
g.yas su zangs bum nyer lnga'i rdzas ldan /
g.yon du chu sbyin snod zangs gzhong sku rten dang bcas pa /
nye logs su chu bum yang bzhag
!
/bal po aHhU~M dzaM nag la /
dkyil 'khor ram tshom bu gtso 'khor dgu
/de rgyab bzhi bkod pa'i dbus su thugs rten thod pa dum gsum nyer lnga sogs kyi bcud ldan nang gsung rten srog 'khor dar gyis dril ba'i rgyab tu sku rten bcas bzhugs /
steng du bum pa chings sngon can /
g.yas su rin chen snod du gtor ma rin chen 'bar ba zas sna bcas /
g.yon du rin chen dar gos /
g.yang rdzas sna tshogs /
rgyab tu mda' dar /
tshe 'brang /
ril chang /

/klong gsal dzaM ser la /

thod chang dang phreng ba /
rdo rje /

/dzaM dmar gnyis /
dzaM nag bcas la tshom bu rang mdog re re /
!
a pa rA dzi ta la tshom bu dmar po bkod /
dbang rdzas ni gzungs dbang gi chas sha stag go
!
/tshogs bdag la tshom bu dmar po /
!
re man+ta la dmar ser /
ku be ra la nag po rnams bkod /
de gsum kar gnam chos chos skyong spyi'i bka' gtad kyi chas so /
!
/dri med gling pa'i pad+ma rgyal po la /
dkyil 'khor ras bris sam /
maN+Dal tshom bu dbus su gtso 'khor lnga de rgyab bzhi bkod pa'i steng /
bum pa nyer lnga'i rdzas ldan chings ser can gtso bo'i sku tsaka gzug pa /
g.yas su dbang gtor /
g.yon du thod chang dar dmar khebs bcas /
rdzas rtags sna bdun tsaka li bcas bkod /
!
dbang gi lha mo mched gsum la /
maN+Dal pad+ma 'dab brgyad mthing ljang dmar po gsum la tshom bu rang mdog bkod pa'i steng gtor ma dkar gsum gyis brgyan cing sku tsaka dar gdugs bcas pa gsum bkod /
sngags byang /
bla rdo /
srog 'khor /

rin po che'i gzhong pa zas snas bkang ba /
dar zab sna tshogs /
nor sna rin po che gang 'dzom bsham /
!
chos rdor dzaM dkar la /
'bru'i pad+ma 'dab brgyad steng gzhung gsal gtor ma dang /
g.yas g.yon tshe ril chang bzhag

/mchog gling bla ma nor lha la /
dkyil 'khor ras bris sam tshom bu dbus su gtso 'khor dgu
/gra bzhi dang sgo bzhir bzhi re bkod pa'i dbus steng khri'ur 'dzom na gzhung mthun bca' sgrub byas pa'i gter bum dang ma 'dzom na gtor ma gzhung mthun /
g.yas su rin po che'i snod du mngar gsum sbyar ba'i chang /

sku gsung thugs dbang sbyor na lha tsaka bcu bdun /
sngags byang /
me long /
rdzas rtags sna bdun bcas bkod /
!
mchog gling rnam sras gcig dril yid bzhin nor bu la /
dkyil 'khor dbus su gtor chen dar gdugs bcas /
de steng many+dzi la bum pa mgul chings mthing nag can /
mdun du sku tsaka sngags byang phyag mtshan gsum gsum gyi tsaka li /
g.yas su rin po che'i snod 'brus bkang bar bla rdo srog 'khor gsum po /
g.yon du zas sna /
dar gos dmar po /
nor sna bcas bzhag
/gtor ma chos sde chen po la ser chen /
spyi la mdung dmar can /
mi dpon la rta sngon can gtsor bya bar gsungs pas dbang gi skabs dmar ser gang rung byas pas 'thus so /
!
/kun 'khyil mched gsum la /
maN+Dal gsum phreng tshar du bsgrigs pa la pad+ma 'dab brgyad ser sngo dmar ba'i lte bar tshom bu re re bkod pa'i steng du many+dzi la thod pa mtshan ldan re re'i nang du 'brang rgyas gtor ma nor gzugs pad sdong can rtse rgyan gser gyi satwa    res mtshan pa la rtswa ku sha'i chun po re btsugs pa la sku tsaka btags pa dar gdugs lha mdog dang mtshungs pa can bkod /
de rnams kyi steng ngam rgyab ngos mtho bar so so'i bum pa bcud ldan yang 'jog
!
/byang gter mnga' dbang rin chen 'bar ba la /

'byung lnga'i gdan /
lha 'dre mi gsum srog yig
/rgyal po'i rtags drug

/klu mi mgon dkar po la /

//rigs rgyud rgyas byed gter gsar rin chen mkha' 'gro la /

//bstan pa rgyas byed sangs gling dang zhig gling lugs kyi gnas bcu'i rjes gnang la /

//de nas dbang gi las kyi skor las /

dar dmar gyi gur phub /

gu ru pad+ma d+hA ki nI sid+d+hi hU~M hrIHmaH

/dgongs gter sgrol ma dmar mo la /

/gter gsar lha chen la /

//de nas drag po mngon spyod kyi skor las /
gtso bo 'joms byed rtsal chen gyi bka' gtad la /
zhing lpags kyi gdan la slob dpon zhal byang shar du bstan te 'khod pa'i g.yas g.yon gnyis su mda' chag grum med pa sum sgro+om gyi khri'u re re'i steng 'bru nag tshogs tshad rjen btags kyi phye la gtor ma zur gsum dmar po'i dpung zur yan la me ri gyen bstan byas pa zangs snod du mda' khri g.yas par bzhag
/gtor ma de 'dra nag po dpung zur man la me ri thur bstan byas pa lcags snod du mda' khri g.yon par bzhag
/so so'i sku tsaka dang dar gdugs rang mdog phub /
de gnyis kyi bar /
rang mdun thod pa zhig gi nang phur byang gzug
/ling+ga dum bur gtubs te spungs pa'i mthar sha btsos pa dang ma btsos pa dum bu chung ngu slob ma re re la brgya phrag re sbyin rgyu 'dang nges bya /
kong zor gru gsum nag po rtsang thur sum tshom btsugs pa /
'ur rdo dang /

gsang thod /
rig tsaka shel rdo ral gri tho ba phur pa ling ga bcas bkod /
!

gzungs dbang chas bkod do //

//de nas lung a nu yo ga'i skor las /
mkha' 'gro kun dga' 'bum pa'i ma rgyud gsang ba lam khyer la /

/de rgyab bzhi /

/shar du dkar po /
lhor ser po /
nub tu dmar po /

/rgyab tu mkha' 'gro'i gtor chen rgyan spros can /
thod pa mtshan ldan chang dang chos sman mngar gsum sbyar ba /
shog dril lnga so sor dar kha dog lngas dril ba /
dar ras cod pan bcas /
!
gter gsar rdo rje bkod pa la /
sta gon rdzas bzhi /

dkyil 'khor ras bris steng ldeng khri rim pa gnyis pa'i 'og mar khro bo'i gsang bum pho mo'i thod pa kha sbyor chang dang so lngas bkang zhing dar mthing dmar gyis bcings pa lcang los brgyan pa dang /
thod pa dum gcig nang yab yum gyi snying po bris pa'i g.yas g.yon du rdo rje dril bus brten pa /
de dag gi mdun du tshe bum mgul chings dmar po can dang tshe 'brang /

'khor lo /

gcan gzan gyi gdan khri /

byang sgor chu gtsang rnams dngos dang ri mor bris pa bzhag
/mdun phyogs su dpal gtor la ri rab gling bzhi 'dod yon bkod pa sna tshogs kyi tsaka li btsugs pa'i g.yas g.yon du sman raka bsham /
gzhan yang dbang rdzas dbu rgyan /
rdo rje /
dril bu rnams dang /
dar lam dkar po'ang 'du bya /
!
yang ti gser gyi 'bru gcig la /
sta gon rdzas bzhi /
ras bris dbus su rnam bum rig dbang chas las ming dbang sna tshogs rdo rje /
lha tsaka tshang ba /
thod chang khar me long dwangs pa bkab pa /
dril bu /
mar me /
rlung g.yab me long shel rdo lhan cig pa rnams bzhag go
!
/mchog gling rigs gsum snying thig las /
dang po lha mi'i theg pa skyab sdom 'bogs pa la /
gnas khang byi dor bya /
dri bzang chus chag chag gdab /
stegs gtsang mar me tog sil ma bkram pa'i dbus su thub pa'i dbang po'i sku brnyan /
g.yas su gsung rab kyi glegs bam /
g.yon du mchod rten rnams snod gcig tu bzhugs /
mdun du phyi mchod phreng tshar du bsham /
nyan rang byang sems yan bskur sgrub dus gcig byed na 'og nas 'byung ba'i gshom rnams kyang stegs bu gcig gi steng gral thabs sam /
phyogs bzhi lta bur bkod /
!
gnyis pa nyan thos theg pa la /
gzhung nas gsal ba ltar 'jam dpal sogs nyan thos tshul bzung ba'i 'bur sku'am tsaka li gsum /
so thar mdo lta bu'i glegs bam /
mchod rten rnams so sor bzhugs /
chu gnyis nyer spyod phreng tshar du bsham /
!
gsum pa rang rgyal theg pa la /
tsan dan dkar pos byugs pa'i maN+Dal gyi steng du gzhung nas bshad pa ltar rigs gsum rang rgyal gyi sku bris 'bur gang rung dang /
phyi mchod bsham /
!
bzhi pa byang sems theg pa la /
dkyil 'khor rta babs med pa'i sgo rkyang khrus rdzing skyed tshal rin po che'i lcags ris bskor ba'i dbus su pad+ma'i gdan sum bsgrigs la rigs gsum byang sems gzhung nas bshad pa lta bu'i sku brnyan nam tsaka li dang /
phyi mchod bsham /
!
lnga pa kr-i ya ste bya ba'i rgyud la /
dkyil 'khor tsan dan dkar po la sogs pa'i dri ldan shing leb kyi gzhi la pad+ma 'dab brgyad sum bsgrigs kyi steng du yod na dbus su 'jam dbyangs /
g.yas su spyan ras gzigs /
g.yon du phyag rdor rnams tsan dkar las byas pa'i sku brnyan nam /
ma 'dzom na tsaka li bzhag
/g.yas g.yon du rnam bum nyer lnga'i bcud ldan kha rgyan gzungs rdor bcas pa /
nor bu'i cod pan /
stod g.yogs dar dpyangs bcas dngos sam ri mor bris pa /
rdzas rtags /
rgyal srid rnams kyi tsaka li /
nyer spyod rnams mdun nas g.yas bskor du bsham /
!
drug pa yo ga la rigs gsum gyi /
dang po 'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa' la /
dkyil 'khor dbus su 'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa'i sku brnyan bris 'bur gang rung bzhugs /
sngags byang ngam phreng ba dang /
phyag mtshan bzhag
/'di'i dbang bskur sger du byed na rnam bum bkod /
phyi mchod bsham /
!
gnyis pa spyan ras gzigs 'khor ba dong sprugs la /
dkyil 'khor dbus su bum pa nyer lnga'i bcud ldan dang sku gzugs bris 'bur gang rung bzhugs /
sngags byang ngam phreng ba /
phyag mtshan bzhag
/phyi mchod bsham /
!
gsum pa gsang bdag ngan song kun 'dren la /
dkyil 'khor dbus su bum pa nyer lnga'i bcud ldan dang /
sku brnyan bris 'bur gang rung bzhugs /
sngags byang ngam phreng ba me long bzhag
/phyi mchod bsham /
!
bdun pa ma hA yo ga 'jam dpal rdo rje la /
zhi dkyil ras bris sam maN+Dal la tshom bu lha grangs bkod pa'i dbus su rnam bum so lnga'i bcud ldan mgul chings ser po kha rgyan dang bcas pa /
g.yas su gsang dbang thod pa mtshan ldan dang /
g.yon du khro bo'i gsang thod khye'u dang bu mo lo bcu drug lon pa'i thod pa kha sbyor gsungs kyang ma rnyed na pho mo'i thod pa kha sbyor /
gnyis ka'i nang chang dang chos sman mngar gsum sbyar bas bkang ba /
rgyab tu khro bo'i dpal gtor sku tsaka dar gdugs mthing gas spras pa /
rig ma dang sgrol ging las gshin gyi tsaka li /
'ja' shel /
mdun du sman raka gtor gsum /
nyer spyod bskor bsham bya /
!
brgyad pa lung a nu yo ga pad+ma gar dbang la /
dkyil 'khor gzhung mthun dbus /
gtor tsaka pad+ma he ru ka dang dar gdugs dmar po /
sgrol ging dmar po ral gri dang phur pa thogs pa brje ba las bsham bkod gzhan rnams 'jam dpal rdo rje ji lta ba bya'o /
!
/dgu pa man ngag rdzogs pa chen po gsang bdag snying thig la /
bsham bkod sngar ltar la dkyil 'khor gzhung mthun dbus /
gtor tsaka badzra he ru ka dang dar gdugs mthing nag
/sgrol ging mthing nag ral gri dang phur pa thogs pa bkod /
!
man ngag la /
thig le lnga tshom dbus mthing shar dkar sogs phyogs mdog can gyi lte bar hU~M sngon po /
shar du oM dkar po /
lhor trAM ser po /
nub tu hrIHdmar po /
byang du AHljang gu
/mthar 'od lnga'i mu khyud kyis bskor ba'i dkyil 'khor steng rnam bum mgul chings sngon po /
kha rgyan gseb tu mda' dar shel phreng me long btags pa dang /
rig ma'i mtshon byed pad+ma dmar po rdo rje dkar pos mtshan pa rnams bkod /
!
bcu pa rigs gsum 'dus pa la /
dkyil 'khor ras bris sam maN+Dal la tshom bu lha grangs bkod pa'i dbus rnam rgyal bum pa /
g.yas g.yon du gsang thod /
rig tsaka brda /
rang byung 'ja' shel rnams dang /
'gro 'dul phrin las kyi dbang chas /
rigs gsum mchod rten lnga pa bris 'bur gang rung 'dzom na dang /
med na mchod rten rab gnas ldan pa /
sangs rgyas kyi ring bsrel dngos dang de nyid phab gtar sbyar nas dril ba'i ril bu /
shes rab ril bu gzhung gsal bsdu bsgrubs byas pa bcas so sor rin po che'i za ma tog la sogs pa'i snod du bzhag pa /
!
tshe dkyil rin po che zur bzhi pa'i dbus su bum pa nyer lnga'i bcud ldan mgul chings dmar po /
tshe ril tshe chang bcas phyogs gang bder bkod /
bka' srung dud sol ma'i rjes gnang 'dir sbrel na bde bas 'og nas bshad pa'i chas rnams mdun phyogs lta bur bsgrig
/sman raka gtor gsum /
nyer spyod kyis mtshon bsham bkod dang nyer mkho snga ma rnams ltar bya'o /
!
/bcu gcig pa bka' srung dud sol ma'i srog gtad la /
'bru nag gi tshom bu'i steng du /
thod pa'am zangs lcags kyi snod du sha khrag gis sbags pa'i gtor ma zur gsum me ri dar gdugs kyis spras pa bkod /
g.yas g.yon du /
sku tsaka
/sngags byang /
dri bzang gi chu /
phyag mtshan bzhi dngos sam bris pa rnams dang /
sman raka nyer spyod spyi ltar bsham /
khrag chang gi skyems /
'bul gtor sogs kyang bsdog
!
/dgongs 'dus pusti lung dbang la /
stegs gtsang mar me tog sil ma bkram pa'i dbus su /
khri stegs la thub dbang sku brnyan byin ldan bzhugs /
g.yas phyogs su theg dgu'i glegs bam rim par gtad du rung bar bzhag dgos pas /
'dul ba so thar mdo dang brgyad stong pa /
mngon pa mdzod tsam /
bya spyod rnal 'byor gsum la bka' 'gyur rgyud 'bum nas pod re tsam mam de dag gi sgrub thabs re tsam dar gyis dril la bzhag
/ma hA yo ga la gter mdzod pod dang po nas mngon spyod las rdzogs kyi bar tshang ma /
a nu la ma rgyud gsang ba lam khyer sogs /
a ti sems sde man chad tshang ba bzhugs /
g.yon du gnas brtan gyi sku gzugs /
mdun du phyi mchod rnam bdun phreng tshar dang maN+Dal rgyas par bsham pas grub bo //
nam mkha'i rnal 'byor rtogs pa'i gding rnyed pas //
sbyangs pa sngon song skal ldan rjes bzung ba //
kun rdzob tsam la ltos pa ma yin kyang //
snyigs dus de 'dra'i snod bcud 'dzom pa dkon //
bden pa gnyis po gcig la gcig brten pa //
chos nyid gshis lugs rten cing 'brel 'byung phyir //
dang po'i las can rgyud smin byed pa la //
mtshan ma'i dkyil 'khor dbang rdzas tshang ba dgos //
rim gnyis rnal 'byor ji bzhin mi brtan kyang //
dam tshig yan lag ci nus tshogs gyur na //
de dang mthun pa'i phan yon 'thob 'gyur bas //
nus pas gang lcogs snyom las dbang ma gtang //
bshad tshod lag len dgos pa dogs pa'i mtha'//
gzhung don ras su bor ba lhod pa'i skyon //
spangs nas 'di tsam 'grub na deng dus kyi //
dbang bskur yin par rloms nas ched du bkod //
'dis kyang rin chen gter gyi mdzod chen po'i //
smin byed sgo 'phar phyogs brgyar dbye ba la //
snang ba'i gzi ldan sgron me nyid gyur nas //
kun rmongs sel zhing legs lam rab gsal shog
/tshul 'di ltar mkhyen rab rgyas pa'i dam pa rnams la mi mkho yang rang 'dra'i blo dman 'chad nyan gyi khur 'dzin pa la rgyus shes lam ston gyi tshul du thugs phan thogs par re ba'i lhag blos kun nas bslangs te mdzod chen gyi glegs bam yongs su rdzogs par grub pa'i rjes thog tu karma ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho phrin las kun khyab dpal bzang po'am /
rgyal ba'i sras po blo gros mtha' yas pa'i sdes de bI ko Ti tsa 'dra rin chen brag gi sgrub gnas su bgyis pa dge legs 'phel /
mang+ga lam //
